It is a paradise for skiing and mountaineering. Visitors can admire Zermatt\u2019s breathtaking views from atop Gornergrat at 3,089m when taking the cable car ride. The traditional wood houses with red rooftops make a memorable impression.\n\nInterlaken\nInterlaken is a popular resort town nestled between two jewel-toned lakes, Thun and Brienz. The fresh air, spectacular natural scenery of snow-capped mountains make it an ideal destination for outdoor activities like hiking, mountain climbing and kayaking. The old towns and tourist caf\u00e9s are also worth exploring.\n\nIn summary, with incredible natural wonders and famous tourist cities, Switzerland will surely give you an unforgettable trip.
